table with random sets each week.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-sql notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"CREATE PROCEDURE UpdateBlackMarketSets()\nBEGIN\n    -- Clear the current sets table\n    DELETE FROM black_market_current_set;\n\n    -- Insert new random sets for each class\n    INSERT INTO black_market_current_set (class, item_set_id, set_name)\n    SELECT class, item_set_id, set_name\n    FROM (\n        SELECT class, item_set_id, set_name,\n               ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY class ORDER BY RAND()) AS rn\n        FROM black_market_armor_sets\n    ) AS temp\n    WHERE temp.rn = 1;\nEND;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003eCREATE PROCEDURE UpdateBlackMarketSets()\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eBEGIN\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e--\u003c/span\u003e Clear the current sets black_market_current_set (class, item_set_id, set_name)\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eSELECT\u003c/span\u003e class, item_set_id, set_name\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eFROM\u003c/span\u003e (\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eSELECT\u003c/span\u003e class, item_set_id, set_name,\n               ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY class \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eORDER BY\u003c/span\u003e RAND()) \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eAS\u003c/span\u003e rn\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eFROM\u003c/span\u003e black_market_armor_sets\n    ) \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eAS\u003c/span\u003e temp\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eWHERE\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSet up the event scheduler to call the stored procedure every week.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-sql notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"SET GLOBAL event_scheduler = ON;\n\nDROP EVENT IF EXISTS UpdateBlackMarketEvent;\n\nCREATE EVENT IF NOT EXISTS UpdateBlackMarketEvent\nON SCHEDULE EVERY 1 WEEK\nDO\n    CALL UpdateBlackMarketSets();\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan dir=\"auto\"\u003eHeres the Lua script that interacts with the above SQL tables. Make sure this script is correctly placed in your servers Lua scripts directory.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"local BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID = 101111 -- Replace with your NPC's ID\nlocal ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID = 910001 -- ID Tokens or Currency\nlocal SET_COST = 100 -- Cost of each armor set in Araxia Tokens\nlocal UPDATE_INTERVAL = 604800 -- 1 week in seconds\n\nlocal CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS = {\n    [11] = {name = \u0026quot;Druid\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_druid\u0026quot;},\n    [3] = {name = \u0026quot;Hunter\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_hunter\u0026quot;},\n    [8] = {name = \u0026quot;Mage\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_mage\u0026quot;},\n    [2] = {name = \u0026quot;Paladin\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_paladin\u0026quot;},\n    [5] = {name = \u0026quot;Priest\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_priest\u0026quot;},\n    [4] = {name = \u0026quot;Rogue\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_rogue\u0026quot;},\n    [7] = {name = \u0026quot;Shaman\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_shaman\u0026quot;},\n    [9] = {name = \u0026quot;Warlock\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_warlock\u0026quot;},\n    [1] = {name = \u0026quot;Warrior\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\classicon_warrior\u0026quot;},\n    [6] = {name = \u0026quot;Death Knight\u0026quot;, icon = \u0026quot;Interface\\\\icons\\\\spell_deathknight_classicon\u0026quot;}\n}\n\nlocal selectedSets = {}\n\nlocal function UpdateBlackMarketSets()\n    selectedSets = {}\n    local query = WorldDBQuery(\u0026quot;SELECT class, item_set_id, set_name FROM black_market_current_set\u0026quot;)\n    if query then\n        repeat\n            local class = query:GetInt32(0)\n            local item_set_id = query:GetInt32(1)\n            local set_name = query:GetString(2)\n            selectedSets[class] = { item_set_id = item_set_id, set_name = set_name }\n        until not query:NextRow()\n    end\nend\n\nUpdateBlackMarketSets()\n\nlocal function BlackMarket_OnGossipHello(event, player, creature)\n    player:GossipClearMenu()\n    for classId, classData in pairs(CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS) do\n        local icon = \u0026quot;|T\u0026quot; .. classData.icon .. \u0026quot;:25|t\u0026quot;\n        player:GossipMenuAddItem(0, icon .. \u0026quot; View \u0026quot; .. classData.name .. \u0026quot; armor set\u0026quot;, 0, classId)\n    end\n    player:GossipSendMenu(1, creature)\nend\n\nlocal function ShowAvailableSets(player, creature, classId)\n    local selectedSet = selectedSets[classId]\n    if selectedSet then\n        local set_name = selectedSet.set_name\n        local item_set_id = selectedSet.item_set_id\n        \n        player:GossipClearMenu()\n        player:GossipMenuAddItem(0, set_name .. \u0026quot; (100 Araxia Tokens)\u0026quot;, 0, 1000 + item_set_id)\n        player:GossipMenuAddItem(0, \u0026quot;Back\u0026quot;, 0, 999) -- Add an option to go back to the class menu\n        player:GossipSendMenu(1, creature)\n    else\n        player:SendNotification(\u0026quot;No set available for this class.\u0026quot;)\n        BlackMarket_OnGossipHello(event, player, creature)\n    end\nend\n\nlocal function BlackMarket_OnGossipSelectOption(event, player, creature, sender, item_set_id, code)\n    local token_count = player:GetItemCount(ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID)\n    if token_count \u0026gt;= SET_COST then\n        local items_query = WorldDBQuery(\u0026quot;SELECT item_id FROM black_market_armor_sets WHERE item_set_id = \u0026quot; .. item_set_id)\n        if items_query then\n            repeat\n                local item_id = items_query:GetInt32(0)\n                player:AddItem(item_id, 1)\n            until not items_query:NextRow()\n        end\n        player:RemoveItem(ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID, SET_COST)\n        player:SendNotification(\u0026quot;You have purchased the armor set for \u0026quot; .. SET_COST .. \u0026quot; Araxia Tokens.\u0026quot;)\n    else\n        player:SendNotification(\u0026quot;You do not have enough Araxia Tokens.\u0026quot;)\n    end\n    player:GossipComplete()\nend\n\nlocal function BlackMarket_OnGossipSelect(event, player, creature, sender, intid, code)\n    if intid == 999 then\n        BlackMarket_OnGossipHello(event, player, creature) -- Go back to the class menu\n    elseif intid \u0026gt;= 1000 then\n        BlackMarket_OnGossipSelectOption(event, player, creature, sender, intid - 1000, code) -- Handle item purchase\n    elseif CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS[intid] then\n        ShowAvailableSets(player, creature, intid) -- Show armor sets for the selected class\n    end\nend\n\nRegisterCreatureGossipEvent(BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID, 1, BlackMarket_OnGossipHello) -- GOSSIP_HELLO\nRegisterCreatureGossipEvent(BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID, 2, BlackMarket_OnGossipSelect) -- GOSSIP_SELECT\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003elocal\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003eBLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 jMJFjm"><section aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eRvpKx"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 cTsUqU js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Black-Market-Vendor</h1><a id="user-content-black-market-vendor" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Black-Market-Vendor" href="#black-market-vendor"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Adds a Vendor who sells 1 Armor Set per class and rotates them out weekly.</p>
<p dir="auto">The SQL table's (<code>black_market_armor_sets</code> <code>black_market_current_set</code>) is created in your "World" folder. The Lua script for the NPC handles randomly getting the Armor sets and allows players to purchase them for 100 Araxia Tokens (Item ID: 910001).</p>
<p dir="auto">One table for all the armor sets and one table for the current sets (resets weekly).
<br>
<br></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 1: Create <code>black_market_armor_sets</code> Table and populate it</h3><a id="user-content-step-1-create-black_market_armor_sets-table-and-populate-it" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 1: Create black_market_armor_sets Table and populate it" href="#step-1-create-black_market_armor_sets-table-and-populate-it"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">(A. Create <code>black_market_armor_sets</code> first and populate it, you can use the SQL provided in this repo.)</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `black_market_armor_sets` (
    `class` INT NOT NULL,
    `item_id` INT NOT NULL,
    `name` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    `item_set_id` INT NOT NULL,
    `set_name` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (`item_id`)
);"><pre><span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> <span class="pl-en">IF</span> NOT EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>black_market_armor_sets<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> (
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>class<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>item_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">255</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>item_set_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>set_name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">255</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span>,
    <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> (<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>item_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>)
);</pre></div>
<br>
<br>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 3: Create <code>black_market_current_set</code> Table</h2><a id="user-content-step-3-create-black_market_current_set-table" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 3: Create black_market_current_set Table" href="#step-3-create-black_market_current_set-table"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This table will hold the current week's selected armor sets for each class.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `black_market_current_set` (
    `class` INT NOT NULL,
    `item_set_id` INT NOT NULL,
    `set_name` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (`class`)
);"><pre><span class="pl-k">CREATE</span> <span class="pl-k">TABLE</span> <span class="pl-en">IF</span> NOT EXISTS <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>black_market_current_set<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> (
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>class<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>item_set_id<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">INT</span> <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>set_name<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span> <span class="pl-k">VARCHAR</span>(<span class="pl-c1">255</span>) <span class="pl-k">NOT NULL</span>,
    <span class="pl-k">PRIMARY KEY</span> (<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>class<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>)
);</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 4: Create the Stored Procedure</h2><a id="user-content-step-4-create-the-stored-procedure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 4: Create the Stored Procedure" href="#step-4-create-the-stored-procedure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The stored procedure will update the <code>black_market_current_set</code> table with random sets each week.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="CREATE PROCEDURE UpdateBlackMarketSets()
BEGIN
    -- Clear the current sets table
    DELETE FROM black_market_current_set;

    -- Insert new random sets for each class
    INSERT INTO black_market_current_set (class, item_set_id, set_name)
    SELECT class, item_set_id, set_name
    FROM (
        SELECT class, item_set_id, set_name,
               ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY class ORDER BY RAND()) AS rn
        FROM black_market_armor_sets
    ) AS temp
    WHERE temp.rn = 1;
END;"><pre>CREATE PROCEDURE UpdateBlackMarketSets()
<span class="pl-k">BEGIN</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Clear the current sets table</span>
    <span class="pl-k">DELETE</span> <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> black_market_current_set;

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Insert new random sets for each class</span>
    <span class="pl-k">INSERT INTO</span> black_market_current_set (class, item_set_id, set_name)
    <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> class, item_set_id, set_name
    <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> (
        <span class="pl-k">SELECT</span> class, item_set_id, set_name,
               ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY class <span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> RAND()) <span class="pl-k">AS</span> rn
        <span class="pl-k">FROM</span> black_market_armor_sets
    ) <span class="pl-k">AS</span> temp
    <span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-c1">temp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">rn</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
END;</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 5: Create the Event Scheduler</h2><a id="user-content-step-5-create-the-event-scheduler" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 5: Create the Event Scheduler" href="#step-5-create-the-event-scheduler"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Set up the event scheduler to call the stored procedure every week.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="SET GLOBAL event_scheduler = ON;

DROP EVENT IF EXISTS UpdateBlackMarketEvent;

CREATE EVENT IF NOT EXISTS UpdateBlackMarketEvent
ON SCHEDULE EVERY 1 WEEK
DO
    CALL UpdateBlackMarketSets();"><pre><span class="pl-k">SET</span> GLOBAL event_scheduler <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">ON</span>;

DROP EVENT IF EXISTS UpdateBlackMarketEvent;

CREATE EVENT IF NOT EXISTS UpdateBlackMarketEvent
<span class="pl-k">ON</span> SCHEDULE EVERY <span class="pl-c1">1</span> WEEK
DO
    CALL UpdateBlackMarketSets();</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 6: Test the Stored Procedure Manually</h2><a id="user-content-step-6-test-the-stored-procedure-manually" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 6: Test the Stored Procedure Manually" href="#step-6-test-the-stored-procedure-manually"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Manually call the stored procedure to ensure it works as expected.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="CALL UpdateBlackMarketSets();"><pre>CALL UpdateBlackMarketSets();</pre></div>
<br>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Lua Script for the NPC</h2><a id="user-content-lua-script-for-the-npc" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Lua Script for the NPC" href="#lua-script-for-the-npc"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Heres the Lua script that interacts with the above SQL tables. Make sure this script is correctly placed in your servers Lua scripts directory.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-lua notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="local BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID = 101111 -- Replace with your NPC's ID
local ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID = 910001 -- ID Tokens or Currency
local SET_COST = 100 -- Cost of each armor set in Araxia Tokens
local UPDATE_INTERVAL = 604800 -- 1 week in seconds

local CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS = {
    [11] = {name = &quot;Druid&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_druid&quot;},
    [3] = {name = &quot;Hunter&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_hunter&quot;},
    [8] = {name = &quot;Mage&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_mage&quot;},
    [2] = {name = &quot;Paladin&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_paladin&quot;},
    [5] = {name = &quot;Priest&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_priest&quot;},
    [4] = {name = &quot;Rogue&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_rogue&quot;},
    [7] = {name = &quot;Shaman&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_shaman&quot;},
    [9] = {name = &quot;Warlock&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_warlock&quot;},
    [1] = {name = &quot;Warrior&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\classicon_warrior&quot;},
    [6] = {name = &quot;Death Knight&quot;, icon = &quot;Interface\\icons\\spell_deathknight_classicon&quot;}
}

local selectedSets = {}

local function UpdateBlackMarketSets()
    selectedSets = {}
    local query = WorldDBQuery(&quot;SELECT class, item_set_id, set_name FROM black_market_current_set&quot;)
    if query then
        repeat
            local class = query:GetInt32(0)
            local item_set_id = query:GetInt32(1)
            local set_name = query:GetString(2)
            selectedSets[class] = { item_set_id = item_set_id, set_name = set_name }
        until not query:NextRow()
    end
end

UpdateBlackMarketSets()

local function BlackMarket_OnGossipHello(event, player, creature)
    player:GossipClearMenu()
    for classId, classData in pairs(CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS) do
        local icon = &quot;|T&quot; .. classData.icon .. &quot;:25|t&quot;
        player:GossipMenuAddItem(0, icon .. &quot; View &quot; .. classData.name .. &quot; armor set&quot;, 0, classId)
    end
    player:GossipSendMenu(1, creature)
end

local function ShowAvailableSets(player, creature, classId)
    local selectedSet = selectedSets[classId]
    if selectedSet then
        local set_name = selectedSet.set_name
        local item_set_id = selectedSet.item_set_id
        
        player:GossipClearMenu()
        player:GossipMenuAddItem(0, set_name .. &quot; (100 Araxia Tokens)&quot;, 0, 1000 + item_set_id)
        player:GossipMenuAddItem(0, &quot;Back&quot;, 0, 999) -- Add an option to go back to the class menu
        player:GossipSendMenu(1, creature)
    else
        player:SendNotification(&quot;No set available for this class.&quot;)
        BlackMarket_OnGossipHello(event, player, creature)
    end
end

local function BlackMarket_OnGossipSelectOption(event, player, creature, sender, item_set_id, code)
    local token_count = player:GetItemCount(ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID)
    if token_count &gt;= SET_COST then
        local items_query = WorldDBQuery(&quot;SELECT item_id FROM black_market_armor_sets WHERE item_set_id = &quot; .. item_set_id)
        if items_query then
            repeat
                local item_id = items_query:GetInt32(0)
                player:AddItem(item_id, 1)
            until not items_query:NextRow()
        end
        player:RemoveItem(ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID, SET_COST)
        player:SendNotification(&quot;You have purchased the armor set for &quot; .. SET_COST .. &quot; Araxia Tokens.&quot;)
    else
        player:SendNotification(&quot;You do not have enough Araxia Tokens.&quot;)
    end
    player:GossipComplete()
end

local function BlackMarket_OnGossipSelect(event, player, creature, sender, intid, code)
    if intid == 999 then
        BlackMarket_OnGossipHello(event, player, creature) -- Go back to the class menu
    elseif intid &gt;= 1000 then
        BlackMarket_OnGossipSelectOption(event, player, creature, sender, intid - 1000, code) -- Handle item purchase
    elseif CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS[intid] then
        ShowAvailableSets(player, creature, intid) -- Show armor sets for the selected class
    end
end

RegisterCreatureGossipEvent(BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID, 1, BlackMarket_OnGossipHello) -- GOSSIP_HELLO
RegisterCreatureGossipEvent(BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID, 2, BlackMarket_OnGossipSelect) -- GOSSIP_SELECT"><pre><span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">101111</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Replace with your NPC's ID</span>
<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">910001</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> ID Tokens or Currency</span>
<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">SET_COST</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">100</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Cost of each armor set in Araxia Tokens</span>
<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">UPDATE_INTERVAL</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">604800</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> 1 week in seconds</span>

<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> {
    [<span class="pl-c1">11</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Druid<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_druid<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">3</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hunter<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_hunter<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">8</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Mage<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_mage<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">2</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Paladin<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_paladin<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">5</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Priest<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_priest<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">4</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Rogue<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_rogue<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">7</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Shaman<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_shaman<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">9</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Warlock<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_warlock<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Warrior<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>classicon_warrior<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
    [<span class="pl-c1">6</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> {<span class="pl-smi">name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Death Knight<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Interface<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>icons<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>spell_deathknight_classicon<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>}
}

<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">selectedSets</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> {}

<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">UpdateBlackMarketSets</span>()
    <span class="pl-smi">selectedSets</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> {}
    <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">query</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">WorldDBQuery</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>SELECT class, item_set_id, set_name FROM black_market_current_set<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-smi">query</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
        <span class="pl-k">repeat</span>
            <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">class</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">query</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GetInt32</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
            <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">item_set_id</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">query</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GetInt32</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
            <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">set_name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">query</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GetString</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)
            <span class="pl-smi">selectedSets</span>[<span class="pl-smi">class</span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> { <span class="pl-smi">item_set_id</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">item_set_id</span>, <span class="pl-smi">set_name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">set_name</span> }
        <span class="pl-k">until</span> <span class="pl-k">not</span> <span class="pl-en">query</span>:<span class="pl-c1">NextRow</span>()
    <span class="pl-k">end</span>
<span class="pl-k">end</span>

<span class="pl-c1">UpdateBlackMarketSets</span>()

<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">BlackMarket_OnGossipHello</span>(<span class="pl-smi">event</span>, <span class="pl-smi">player</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>)
    <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GossipClearMenu</span>()
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">classId</span>, <span class="pl-smi">classData</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">pairs</span>(<span class="pl-smi">CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS</span>) <span class="pl-k">do</span>
        <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>|T<span class="pl-pds">" </span></span><span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-smi">classData</span>.<span class="pl-e">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>:25|t<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GossipMenuAddItem</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">icon</span> <span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> View <span class="pl-pds">" </span></span><span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-smi">classData</span>.<span class="pl-e">name</span> <span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> armor set<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">classId</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">end</span>
    <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GossipSendMenu</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>)
<span class="pl-k">end</span>

<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">ShowAvailableSets</span>(<span class="pl-smi">player</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>, <span class="pl-smi">classId</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">selectedSet</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">selectedSets</span>[<span class="pl-smi">classId</span>]
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-smi">selectedSet</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
        <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">set_name</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">selectedSet</span>.<span class="pl-e">set_name</span>
        <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">item_set_id</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">selectedSet</span>.<span class="pl-e">item_set_id</span>
        
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GossipClearMenu</span>()
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GossipMenuAddItem</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">set_name</span> <span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> (100 Araxia Tokens)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1000</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">item_set_id</span>)
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GossipMenuAddItem</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Back<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">999</span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Add an option to go back to the class menu</span>
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GossipSendMenu</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">SendNotification</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>No set available for this class.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
        <span class="pl-c1">BlackMarket_OnGossipHello</span>(<span class="pl-smi">event</span>, <span class="pl-smi">player</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">end</span>
<span class="pl-k">end</span>

<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">BlackMarket_OnGossipSelectOption</span>(<span class="pl-smi">event</span>, <span class="pl-smi">player</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>, <span class="pl-smi">sender</span>, <span class="pl-smi">item_set_id</span>, <span class="pl-smi">code</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">token_count</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GetItemCount</span>(<span class="pl-smi">ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-smi">token_count</span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;=</span> <span class="pl-smi">SET_COST</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
        <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">items_query</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">WorldDBQuery</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>SELECT item_id FROM black_market_armor_sets WHERE item_set_id = <span class="pl-pds">" </span></span><span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-smi">item_set_id</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-smi">items_query</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
            <span class="pl-k">repeat</span>
                <span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-smi">item_id</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">items_query</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GetInt32</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
                <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">AddItem</span>(<span class="pl-smi">item_id</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
            <span class="pl-k">until</span> <span class="pl-k">not</span> <span class="pl-en">items_query</span>:<span class="pl-c1">NextRow</span>()
        <span class="pl-k">end</span>
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">RemoveItem</span>(<span class="pl-smi">ARAXIA_TOKEN_ID</span>, <span class="pl-smi">SET_COST</span>)
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">SendNotification</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>You have purchased the armor set for <span class="pl-pds">" </span></span><span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-smi">SET_COST</span> <span class="pl-k">..</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> Araxia Tokens.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
        <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">SendNotification</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>You do not have enough Araxia Tokens.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
    <span class="pl-k">end</span>
    <span class="pl-en">player</span>:<span class="pl-c1">GossipComplete</span>()
<span class="pl-k">end</span>

<span class="pl-k">local</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">BlackMarket_OnGossipSelect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">event</span>, <span class="pl-smi">player</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>, <span class="pl-smi">sender</span>, <span class="pl-smi">intid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">code</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-smi">intid</span> <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">999</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">BlackMarket_OnGossipHello</span>(<span class="pl-smi">event</span>, <span class="pl-smi">player</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Go back to the class menu</span>
    <span class="pl-k">elseif</span> <span class="pl-smi">intid</span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1000</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">BlackMarket_OnGossipSelectOption</span>(<span class="pl-smi">event</span>, <span class="pl-smi">player</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>, <span class="pl-smi">sender</span>, <span class="pl-smi">intid</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1000</span>, <span class="pl-smi">code</span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Handle item purchase</span>
    <span class="pl-k">elseif</span> <span class="pl-smi">CLASS_NAMES_AND_ICONS</span>[<span class="pl-smi">intid</span>] <span class="pl-k">then</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">ShowAvailableSets</span>(<span class="pl-smi">player</span>, <span class="pl-smi">creature</span>, <span class="pl-smi">intid</span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Show armor sets for the selected class</span>
    <span class="pl-k">end</span>
<span class="pl-k">end</span>

<span class="pl-c1">RegisterCreatureGossipEvent</span>(<span class="pl-smi">BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-smi">BlackMarket_OnGossipHello</span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> GOSSIP_HELLO</span>
<span class="pl-c1">RegisterCreatureGossipEvent</span>(<span class="pl-smi">BLACK_MARKET_NPC_ID</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-smi">BlackMarket_OnGossipSelect</span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> GOSSIP_SELECT</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Summary of Setup</h3><a id="user-content-summary-of-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Summary of Setup" href="#summary-of-setup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Tables:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>black_market_armor_sets</code>: Contains all possible armor sets and items.</li>
<li><code>black_market_current_set</code>: Contains the current week's selected armor sets.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Stored Procedure:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>UpdateBlackMarketSets</code>: Updates the current sets table with one random armor set per class each week.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Event Scheduler:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>UpdateBlackMarketEvent</code>: Calls the stored procedure weekly to refresh the available sets.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Lua Script:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Manages the NPC interactions, displays the current sets, and handles purchases.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">By following these steps, you ensure that the Black Market NPC is correctly set up to provide players with a weekly rotating selection of armor sets.</p>
